    	var m_randomID = null;

		function OnMouseOver(cntrl) {
    		m_randomID = Math.random();
    		SwitchImage(m_randomID, cntrl.getAttribute('id'), 0, true);
    	}

    	function OnMouseOut(cntrl) {
    		SwitchImage(m_randomID, cntrl.getAttribute('id'), 0, false);
    		m_randomID = 0;
    	}

    	function SwitchImage(randomID, imageID, idx, keepGoing) {
    		if (imageID != null && imageID.length > 0 && randomID == m_randomID) {
    			var currentImage = document.getElementById(imageID);
				if(currentImage==null || currentImage == undefined)
				{
					return;
				}
    			var lst = currentImage.getAttribute('UrlList').split(',');
				
				if(lst == null || lst == undefined) {
					return;
				}
    			if (idx < lst.length) {
    				currentImage.src = lst[idx];
    			}

    			if (keepGoing) {
    				idx++;
    				if (idx >= lst.length) {
    					idx = 0;
    				}

    				var func = "SwitchImage(" + randomID + ",'" + imageID + "'," + (idx + 1) + ", true)";

    				window.setTimeout(func, 1000);
    			}
    		}
    	}

	$(document).ready(function () {
		$('.recordsperpage select').change(function () {
			loc = window.location.href.replace(/\/records[0-9]+/gi, "");
			loc = loc.split("?");
			l = ""; q = "";
			if (loc.length > 0)
				l = loc[0];
			if (loc.length > 1)
				q = "?" + loc[1];
			window.location = l + "records" + $(this).val() + "/" + q;
		});
	});

<script type="text/javascript">
	var clickeditem;
	function DoSearch(clickedid) {
		clickeditem = $('#'+ clickedid);
		var inputBox = clickeditem.parent().find('.search')[0];
		var SearchText = inputBox.value;
		if (IsMobile === undefined) var IsMobile = window.location.href.indexOf("/mobile/") > -1;
		SearchText = SearchText.replace(/[+]/g, "[PLUS]").replace(/[\\]/g, " ");
		var appendExisting = $(inputBox).data('appendexistingsearch');
		var queryString = '{"InventoryType":"U"}';
		$.ajax({
			type: "POST",
			contentType: "application/json; charset=utf-8",
			dataType: "json",
			data: "{SearchText:'" + SearchText + "',isMobile:'" + IsMobile + "',queryString:'" + queryString + "',appendExistingSearch:'" + appendExisting + "'}",
			url: "/TextSearch.asmx/DoSearch",
			success: function (data) {
				if (data.d) {
					window.location = data.d;
				}
				else {
					if (IsMobile) {
						FindControl(clickeditem).parent().parent().find('#SearchMessage').text("No results found");
					}
					else {
						var searchMessage = $('#SearchMessage');
						if (searchMessage.length > 0) {
							searchMessage.text("No results found");
						}
						else {
							alert("No results found");
						}
					}
				}
			}
		});
	}
	</script>
</div>
		</div>
	</div>

	var clickeditem;
	function DoSearch(clickedid) {
		clickeditem = $('#'+ clickedid);
		var inputBox = clickeditem.parent().find('.search')[0];
		var SearchText = inputBox.value;
		if (IsMobile === undefined) var IsMobile = window.location.href.indexOf("/mobile/") > -1;
		SearchText = SearchText.replace(/[+]/g, "[PLUS]").replace(/[\\]/g, " ");
		var appendExisting = $(inputBox).data('appendexistingsearch');
		var queryString = '{"InventoryType":"U"}';
		$.ajax({
			type: "POST",
			contentType: "application/json; charset=utf-8",
			dataType: "json",
			data: "{SearchText:'" + SearchText + "',isMobile:'" + IsMobile + "',queryString:'" + queryString + "',appendExistingSearch:'" + appendExisting + "'}",
			url: "/TextSearch.asmx/DoSearch",
			success: function (data) {
				if (data.d) {
					window.location = data.d;
				}
				else {
					if (IsMobile) {
						FindControl(clickeditem).parent().parent().find('#SearchMessage').text("No results found");
					}
					else {
						var searchMessage = $('#SearchMessage');
						if (searchMessage.length > 0) {
